<div class="row oprograma">
    <div class="col-md-8 col-xs-12">
        <h2 class="title">O Programa</h2>
        <br />

        <div style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: 0px 0px; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; color: #333333;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: Arial; font-size: small; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;"><span color="#333333" face="Arial" size="2" style="color: #333333; font-family: Arial; font-size: small;">Exibido aos s&aacute;bados, &agrave;s 23 h, o Mega Senha &eacute; um teste de conhecimento, racioc&iacute;nio r&aacute;pido e trabalho em equipe.</span></span></div>
<div style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: 0px 0px; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; color: #333333;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: Arial; font-size: small; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;"><span color="#333333" face="Arial" size="2" style="color: #333333; font-family: Arial; font-size: small;"></span></span></div>
<div id="int_left" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-image: initial; background-position: 0px 0px; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; color: #333333;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: Arial; font-size: small; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;">Dois times, cada um formado por uma celebridade e um participante, numa divertida e emocionante disputa para mostrar quem tem o melhor vocabul&aacute;rio. Esse &eacute; o&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: bold; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 13px; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;"><em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;">Mega Senha</em>,</span>&nbsp;<em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 13px; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;">game show</em>&nbsp;da RedeTV!.</span>
<p align="justify" style="margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: Arial; font-size: small; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;">Na primeira etapa do jogo &ndash; composta de quatro rodadas eliminat&oacute;rias &ndash; um dos membros da dupla d&aacute; dicas para que o outro descubra qual &eacute; a palavra secreta (a Mega Senha) daquela rodada. O participante que acertar o maior n&uacute;mero de palavras ao final das Rodadas Eliminat&oacute;rias passa para a etapa seguinte.</span></p>
<p align="justify" style="margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: Arial; font-size: small; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;">A segunda etapa do jogo consiste em seis rodadas, nas quais a dupla precisa acertar cinco Mega Senhas em um minuto e meio. A cada rodada, o desafio fica maior, j&aacute; que o n&uacute;mero de Mega Senhas vai diminuindo. Se no primeiro&nbsp;<em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 13px; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;">round</em>&nbsp;o time precisa acertar cinco Mega Senhas dentre dez dispon&iacute;veis, no sexto e &uacute;ltimo&nbsp;<em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 13px; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;">round</em>&nbsp;&ndash; valendo o pr&ecirc;mio m&aacute;ximo do programa &ndash; s&atilde;o apenas cinco palavras dispon&iacute;veis e<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: bold; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 13px; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;">todas</span>&nbsp;tem que ser adivinhadas corretamente.</span></p>
<p align="justify" style="margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: Arial; font-size: small; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;">O&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: bold; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 13px; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;"><em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;">Password</em>&nbsp;</span>&ndash; nome original do&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: bold; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 13px; vertical-align: baseline; background: 0px 0px;">Mega Senha</span>&nbsp;&ndash; &eacute; sucesso de p&uacute;blico na Am&eacute;rica do Norte, na Europa e na &Aacute;sia. Agora, ele chega ao Brasil, numa parceria entre a FremantleMedia e a RedeTV!.</span></p>
</div>

        <h2 class="title">Mariana Godoy Entrevista</h2>
        <a href="#" onclick="javascript:window.history.back(); return false;" class="back">VOLTAR</a>
        <div class="clearfix"></div>
        <div class="player embed-responsive embed-responsive-16by9">
            <iframe src="http://mais.uol.com.br/static/uolplayer/?mediaId=16173354&autoplay=true" allowfullscreen="true" webkitallowfullscreen="true" mozallowfullscreen="true" allowfullscreen frameborder="0" ></iframe>
        </div>
        <h3>&quot;Escrevo e mostro as m&#250;sicas para minha m&#227;e&quot;, revela rapper Hungria</h3>
        <p><p>Nascido em Bras&iacute;lia, o cantor e compositor Hungria falou sobre suas m&uacute;sicas que exaltam brincadeiras como carrinho de rolim&atilde; e pipa. "Hoje as crian&ccedil;as s&oacute; ficam no universo tecnol&oacute;gico", disse ele, que admitiu que as redes sociais impulsionaram seu trabalho. Hungria explicou que come&ccedil;ou as escrever m&uacute;sicas muito novo e contou que at&eacute; hoje mostra as composi&ccedil;&otilde;es para sua m&atilde;e: "Viajo muito nessa ideia da cria&ccedil;&atilde;o da m&uacute;sica. Quando escrevo corro para mostrar as m&uacute;sicas para minha m&atilde;e".</p></p>
        <span class="date-item"><strong>Publicada:</strong>
            24/03/2017</span>
